"SOC" stands for Sampler Occurrence Code.  It distinguishes between different samplers of the same type at a site at the same time. This is a user defined code that once assigned should not be changed.
"AQS Code" is a unique code for the site.  It is a combination of the state FIPS code, county FIPS code and the site EPA code.
